# Toronto-area GoingToCamp — sites with electrical outlets

_Generated 2026-05-26 06:24_  
_Scope: rec-areas [1, 4, 8] within ~200 km of Toronto, every Fri-Sun weekend plus the two long weekends until 2026-09-30._

## How to read this report

- **Outlet data** comes from each tenant's `/api/resourcelocation/resources` JSON endpoint, decoded against `/api/attribute/filterable`. Only sites whose **Electrical Service** attribute is set to 15 A or 30 A are listed.
- **Sort order:** weekends chronologically; within each weekend, campgrounds are sorted by a curated subjective score (view + trails + location, 1–5 each, averaged). GoingToCamp does not publish user ratings, so this ranking reflects general reputation for the Toronto-area conservation areas; see the script for the table.
- **Long weekends** (Sat-Mon, 3 nights) are listed in addition to their parent Fri-Sun weekend, not instead of it.
- Each **Book** link opens the booking results page on the correct date range.

## Rec-area summary

| Rec area | Subjective rating (V/T/L) | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| **Long Point Region, Ontario** (#1) | 3 / 3 / 4 | Lake Erie / Carolinian Canada — easy GTA access, mild terrain. |
| **Maitland Valley, Ontario** (#4) | 3 / 3 / 2 | Maitland River valleys — quieter, longer drive from GTA. |
| **Algonquin Highlands** (#8) | 5 / 5 / 3 | Haliburton Highlands — best scenery / hiking of the set; ~3 hr drive. |

> _**Rec-area 5 (Saugeen Valley)** was skipped: its tenant subdomain `saugeen.goingtocamp.com` is not currently resolving upstream._
> _**Rec-area 8 (Algonquin Highlands)** is in scope but produced 0 outlet matches: its two campgrounds (Frost Centre Area, Poker Lakes Area) are interior canoe-camping zones and do not expose an Electrical Service attribute — those sites genuinely have no hookups._
